<Response>None</Response>< review>
This is a nice, clean, and beautiful beach.
Things to know:
DOGS! YES! AND OFF LEASH so pups will be happy here.
Small amount of parking available.
Parking was free in the 2hr section.
Restaurant at entrance,  a little pricy ,but great. Get the calamari.

The beach is enclosed by rock face hills.
So much fun had here.

You will love it!</review>

<userid>115630027673852099033< /userid><name>John Petrovich<//name><time>1593372965373</time><Rating>5</Rating>< Review>
Great Dog beach.... Off leash, dramatic cliffs, not crowded. There's a parking lot and restaurant at the north end, a 200 step stairway down the cliff at the south end. Make sure you check the tide tables though, the beach shortens up quite a bit at high tide, leaving less room for the doggos to run around.<//Review>

</record></dataset><record>
< user>
103583426517654603359< /user>
< Text>
I should be clear, this is for the Boathouse Restaurant: I've been coming here for many years, and this was the best experience I have had. We were anxious when we arrived as the beach and the restaurant were packed, and a lot of folks weren't wearing masks. However within 20 minutes (the exact wait time we were told to expect), we were lucky enough to be seated outside the patio area along the walk in front of the restaurant, well separated from other tables and people. We had a surprisingly good, interesting cocktail, followed by an amazing seafood platter...the middle size was perfect for 2 for a meal, and everything was very fresh and delicious. A lot of variety as well...clams, mussels, oysters, shrimp, crab legs, ceviche, poke. My only very small complaint was the amount of lettuce/cabbage the ceviche sat on in proportion to the amount of ceviche. While it is not inexpensive, I did think it was fairly priced for the quality and quantity. Their wine selection was quite good, with some nice and unexpected local selections. We had a favorite Sauvignon Blanc from a relatively small producer and it was surprisingly reasonably priced. I appreciate this; knowing a bit about wine and retail costs, i get very frustrated when restaurants jack up the prices unreasonably high... it's the difference between them selling me a glass or a bottle, so worth keeping the prices appropriate.  The service was really good...our server was experienced, very polite and warm but professional. She was knowledgeable about the menu, and when asked, she articulately expressed her opinions, which I VERY much appreciate in a server who really knows the menu. She guided us perfectly. We also didn't feel rushed despite it being a fairly busy evening. Quite honestly, I've always come here for the location in the past, but after this experience I will be returning more frequently for the food and beverages. Overall an outstanding experience.</Text>

<Text>I grew up near here and spent a lot of time at Hendry's as a kid.  Now i spend a lot of time here with my own children.  We love it here....our "locals" beach.  Also known as The Pit to a of us long time Santa Barbarans.  One side is off leash dog friendly the other is on leash walking.  Lots of tidepools at low tide.  Parking cam definitely be a challenge especially on a beautiful day.  There is a restaurant ( The Boathouse) on this beach which also makes parking a challenge.  Famy friendly beach.  It does get crowded at times but you can usually find a spot even on the most crowded days.  Can be foggy from time to time eben when there is no fog anywhere else.  Can usually see dolphins out in the water, birds diving for fish, etc.  A great local hangout!<//Text>< GmapID>

<Pictures>None<//Pictures>< Text>
For a long time I thought that this was the only Post Office in the area.
It USED to be very good, and the people that worked there were always friendly and helpful. In fact, I would go there almost every weekend to buy a stamp for my collection.
I stopped collecting when a young me was faced with rude and disgusting behavior. There's just things you don't say to children, and it's stayed with me into adulthood.

I've hated having to come here for nearly 15 years after that incident, but luckily that ended about 4 months ago I found the Huntington Park branch. Not only is it closer to where I live and on my way to one of my jobs, but the people that work there are so nice! It made me realize how terrible this one was.

This Post Office gets one star because they are open on Saturday with limited hours.
Though, I will NEVER be back after what happened to me last weekend.
I was attempting to mail an international package, and there were no custom forms out. So, I waited in line and spoke to an attendant. They insisted I didn't need a customs form on an international package. I said that it was proper protocol, as I mailed out packages like these at least four times a week. Five minutes of this back and forth later I had customs forms flung at me and was told "Fine. Let's see if they get there or not." Her tone indicated that she had no intention of letting my package get to its destination because I was ruining her day with the extra information a customs form required or something.

I didn't even risk it.
I took the forms, notified my customer that their package would be delayed, and went home.

Don't go here unless you're in a dire hurry.
They treat you like dirt on the bottom of their shoe.</Text>

<userid>108636747783816733213<//userid></record></dataset><record>
<name>Matthew Jakubczak</name><Review>This place has become my family's favorite go-to for a good Christmas dinner. While I typically deplore the idea of making anyone work on such a holiday, I am not going to turn down a family dinner, and this place has earned our business 3 years running. The food is always very, very fresh. The ingredients are all very well picked, fresh, and you can taste the quality as opposed to many others. When going for Chinese lately it seems that Panda Express is about the level of quality you can expect in most places, where you can tell the meat is drowned in sauce to try and cover up the fact it is low quality, but not here. As far as I can tell, all the ingredients are what would be a first round choice, and they don't simply try to hide the flaws the meat or veggies may have by covering them with excessive sauce or a crunchy outer shell.

The actual restaurant has downsized a little from the first time we went, which unfortunately without a reservation could mean you will be stuck waiting for another party to finish before you can be seated. But the actual food os worth the wait, and while they don't blatantly rush you through your meal, they will make sure you're satisfied in a timely manner so they may serve other customers. We did not feel rushed, our drinks were kept full, and the food came relatively quickly, which made it easier to eat then go tour the Christmas lights around town. Even with the downsizing, the dining area was not cramped; in fact it seemed like the tables were spread out a little better adding to the comfort for the meal.

The menu is very comprehensive, guaranteed to have something for everyone, with pictures and actual brief descriptions so you arent left totally guessing what is what. I chose the Crispy Beef, which is similar albeit much better than Panda Express' Beijing Beef. The difference that stood out to me was the fact there were good chunks of beef, and what I assume was a rice wine vinegar in the sauce that gave it an almost pickled taste that really worked well.

If you are looking for a quality Chinese place around town, you surely cannot go wrong giving Panda Country a try.< /Review>< Pictures>
None<//Pictures>

<rate>2< /rate>< text>
I had a package delivery attempt made to my house. Calling their telephone number and getting an operator on the phone is tricky. There's no initial option for speaking with an operator even if you keep saying, "Operator." I had to 1st track my package, 2nd tell the automated machine that a second delivery attempt the following day would not work for me, and 3rd finally be connected to a live operator to tell her that I'd rather pick up the package that evening. It was also difficult to understand the operator's English. I'm not very picky and do well with accents but this one was frustrating. Bottom line: if you want to talk to an operator say, "track package," say your tracking number, and wait for the information. Then when the operator tells you that a second attempt will be made the next day, is this okay? Say, "No." You will be connected with a live operator. Note that this works when there has been an unsuccessful delivery attempt. I'm not quite sure how it would work if the package was still out for delivery.</text>

< Text>
The only place we will go for both my husband and my 1 year old! My husband has had 3 different barbers cut his hair here and they all did a PERFECT job!

They will be going to Kevin regularly... he was extremely patient (& is a natural with kids- always trying to make him laugh and keep him happy) with my 1 year old both times he got it cut and he took his time to make sure it was perfect!! I honestly have no clue how he made my baby's hair look so good with how much my little man moved around. Very reasonable price for top notch kids hair cuts, so if your little one is extra difficult, make sure to tip him well!!! My husband's hair turns out perfectly every time, it is worth the extra money (over a super cuts) ANY day. I couldn't be any happier with this place & the job Kevin did!!!

Just a heads up, they do take walk ins but it's a long wait.... they have this great app that tells you where you're at in line and they call your cell phone when they're ready for you. It is TOTALLY worth the wait! You can always schedule an appointment as well, but our schedule is a little hectic so we usually just go in to get "in line" and do some shopping & lunch til it's our turn!<//Text>

<text>AMAZING. I can't believe I lived here 5.5 years and never knew I was 5 minutes from this place. I got the 2 egg and cheese khachapuri, spicy cheese burek, & soujouk and cheese specialty burek. Insane. I asked for the eggs to be runny because I needed it to-go, and it was cooked so perfectly that by the time I got home, my khachapuri was BEAUTIFUL. The 3 items I got were so big that they lasted me 5 meals! I wish I had taken a photo of the soujouk burek. It had so much cheese and meat in it, just a perfect middle eastern "calzone."

Khachapuri and other items are made fresh. Hence, yes, you have to wait if you're going to order them, 15-20 minutes. They have ready-to-eat items like the burek, stuffed grape leaves, etc., if you're in a rush. However, take my advice and wait for the fresh stuff. I could eat here every day.< /text></record></dataset><record>

<date>1416427430080</date>< review>
As a music teacher, OTM is the absolute best. Pasadena is soooo lucky to have a store of this caliber in our community. Even if you're not directly in Pasadena, it's worth the drive to buy everything you need and browse through all the beautiful (Henle!) editions. The store has almost every book imaginable that you would ever need, both as a teacher and as a student. Many of my students opt to shop here instead of ordering online because of the store experience. Knowledgeable people work there, helping with instrumental rentals and book purchases. The owner was a Suzuki piano teacher professionally for many years, and is an absolute joy to communicate with all things music. Cheers :)< /review>
